<Date>1603831786581< /Date>< username>
John Mazurek</username>
< Review>
Many of the recycling centers in Temecula have closed and I searched to find a replacement. SA is a great place to take your cans and plastic bottles.
It can be a bit intimidating but not to worry, just go to the second entrance marked for cans and bottles and pull INDOORS. Yes it out of the sun and in  a large warehouse type of building. Park your car and get a cart and some empty plastic barrels and load up your cans,plastic etc . Wheel them over to the weight station and very friendly and helpful staff weigh your recycling. Then you get a receipt and go to the corner office a get your cash. In my opinion, the rate of pay was very fair. Highly recommend!
They also do a lot more than just cans and bottles, check out their web site for all the materials that they recycle.
Went back for another visit and was pleased with the great service. I was amazed that there was as many women as men recycling. I guess every one can use an extra buck. Every one had masks so I felt safe. The only thing that I found to be a new rule was all caps had to be removed from the plastic bottles, I had to get out of line and spend 10 minutes removing bottle caps. Also the times for returns of CRV materials is 8 am to 1 PM Monday - Sat. See my photo of Rules< /Review>

<name>Scott Mckray<//name>< text>
While service performed was decent, service advisor's attitude was less than adequate. After explaining that my Triumph had been purchased (used) in the spring, I had stripped it down and done some performance modifications and just returned from a 4,000 mi. roadtrip with no problems. Just wanted to do the 24,000 mi major a little early before winter, as I wasn't sure of the previous services other than oil, filter, plugs, wires, and coils I did prior to trip. No notes were written down. I was told they would determine what was to be done, completely discounting what I had just told him. Upon pickup plugs changed unnecessarily and not replaced with iridiums as we're in it. I had to ask for old plugs (4,000 miles) back. 1 K&N pod oiled properly 1 inadequately oiled. Tech lost a hex screw and replaced it with non matching which cracked plastic housing it was meant to hold. Once home I corrected these shortcomings myself. The bulk of the work was performed adequately however advisor's poor attitude will most likely cause me to go either to Elk Grove or to CalMoto in Livermore. A shame that an attitude will outweigh decent (probably very good) mechanical service.</text>

< text>
TLDR:
No wait at prime time on Saturday night
Staff seemed confused and unorganized
Had to add salt to my dish, which I can't recall ever having done

I had higher expectations, but I suppose I should have known this wasn't really going to be the best when there wasn't a wait at prime dinner time on a Saturday night. Not to say the place wasn't busy. The hostess and servers seemed confused and not very organized. After our menus were brought, and man put water on the other end of the table from us, that we dragged towards our place settings. When our server arrived about 15 minutes after we were seated, he simply asked, "Do you know what you want?" While he wasn't rude, and was attentive and friendly for the rest of the meal, it's not the norm at a "white table cloth" restaurant. Our food arrived in an appropriate time after we ordered. I had to add salt to my food. I do not like salty food, and I actually don't even own a salt shaker in my house, but the spaghetti carbonara lacked any flavor, what so ever. The most flavorful part of the dish were the english peas. My partner also  begrudgingly added salt to his meal, because the tomato sauce was flat and tasteless. We didn't have any cocktails, and after the dinner skipped dessert.</text>

<Text>My wife and I love this place. It has been our haven to get out-and-about especially during this pandemic. This place has endured many changes in operation due to the pandemic, so we have visited often and tried to tip well for the hard-working and pleasant staff. They have a menu with a wide selection of offerings: apps, salads, wings, many different, thin-crust pizzas, deserts, and non-alcoholic beverages. They also offer many draft craft brews which change at times, so there is a lot to choose from. They run a lot of specials, like a family "bundle" of food and specials on certain beers every week on I think Tuesdays. They have nice outdoor seating, and when allowed, indoor seating, all very nice/comfortable/clean. If you like pizza and have never tried this place, you should. They do deliver as well!< /Text>< gmap_id>

Stopped in for lunch to try this new "Best" Pizza and Brew location.
Came in with a bit of reserve just because of name that includes "Best"! Not an easy hipe to live up to.....So here we go...
Staff is friendly, nice, and attentive.
Bathroom is clean, two Male, two Female rooms...
Inside is very open, and tends more toward large parties. (Not romantic location..), they even have nice small location for a private party of about 8.
Most pizza choices are similar elsewhere, so I can compare....Decided to eat one slice (Meat Lovers) in restaurant, and get for most part, one of each type available...so 6 slices to go...
Meat-Lover (it is Valentine's Day!)
Specialty of the Day
The White
Pesto Goat
Works
BBQ Chicken
(Extra slice given, Pepperoni...Weee!)
Pizza is very good...will return again!
Come on down......price is reasonable fir sure.....< /Text>

<Name>T J</Name><text>Had dinner at P.F. Chang's in Roseville for the first time. There were several reviews about the wait for food but we figured it was just a one off situation... nope it wasn't. We waited 10 minutes for a table but we had a reservation while other were waiting for 30 minutes.

We were seated and it took 10 minutes to order drinks and 10 more to get them. Once we had our drinks we order appetizers that took 30 minutes. 10 minutes after we ordered apps, we order our dinner. It took them another 30 minutes after our appetizers were served for the dinner to come out. From the time we were seated, it was an hour and 20 minutes for our dinner.

The edemame had very little sea salt which made them bland. The lobster roll was bland until I added some wasabi. The dinners were lacking flavor also. I'm not sure if you have been to Pei Wei but it is like P.F. Chang's and cheaper. Pei Wei flavor are more robust so I was expecting P.F. Chang's to be comparable or better, it wasn't.

The lemon chicken recipe has changed...no longer bite-sized pieces of chicken in a great lemon sauce, but whole breast pieces overwhelmed with Chinese 5-spice powder, who would guess it was supposed to be lemon!   We used to love P.F. Chang's.   What happened???< /Text>
